  <script>
   // register PAGES USABLE metric as depending on the event published when the forms are ready to interect with them
        require(['uitk', 'universalTypeahead'], function(uitk) {

          function markPageUsable() {
            ewe_performance.markPageUsable();
            if (console && typeof console.timeStamp === 'function') {
              console.timeStamp('mark page usable');
            }
          }

          function determineMarkPageUsableStrategy() {
            if(window.requestAnimationFrame && typeof window.requestAnimationFrame === 'function') {
              window.requestAnimationFrame(markPageUsable);
            } else {
              markPageUsable();
            }
          }

          if(window.mercuryFormsInitialized === true) {
            determineMarkPageUsableStrategy();
          } else {
              uitk.subscribe('mercuryForms.initialized', function(topic, obj) {
                determineMarkPageUsableStrategy();
                uitk.unsubscribe('mercuryForms.initialized');
              });
          }
        })
  </script>

             <script type="text/javascript">
              require(['gc/pageModel', 'jquery', 'dctk/dctk'], function (pageModel, $, dctk) {
        var user = pageModel.user;
        var site = pageModel.site;
        var modE2EWhiteRecognisedNonUSExpId = 24998;
        var modE2EWhiteRecognisedUSExpId = 16349;
        var userType = (user) ? user.userStatus : undefined;
        if (userType === 'Identified' || userType === 'AUTHENTICATED') {
            if ('true' === window.modRebrandingExperimentEnabledNonUS) {
                evaluateExperiment(modE2EWhiteRecognisedNonUSExpId);
            } else if ('true' === window.memberOnlyDealsEnabled) {
                evaluateExperiment(modE2EWhiteRecognisedUSExpId);
            }
            else {
                $('.member-pricing-wizard-message').show();
            }
        }

        function evaluateExperiment(experimentId) {
            dctk.evaluateExperimentAndLog({
                id: experimentId,
                guid: pageModel.user.guid,
                tpid: pageModel.site.tpid,
                eapid: pageModel.site.eapid,
                callback: function (experiment) {
                    if (experiment.value === 0) {
                        $('.member-pricing-wizard-message').show();
                    }
                }
            });
        }

    })
             </script>

        function ABTest(childId, validToLog, useControl, controlValues) {
            this.child = childId;
            this.validToLog = validToLog;
            this.value = parseInt(window.serverABTests['ab' + this.child], 10);
            if(isNaN(this.value)){
                this.value = -1;
            }
            this.useControlMarquee = useControl === true && ( controlValues.length === 0 || controlValues.indexOf(this.value) >= 0 );
            this.cmptst = this.child + '.' + this.value;
        }

   (function (undefined) {

        function trackExperiments (perfTracking) {
            require('dctk/dctk', function (dctk) {
                if (dctk && dctk.ewePerformance && (typeof dctk.ewePerformance.addData === 'function')) {
                    for (var experimentId in perfTracking) {
                        if (perfTracking.hasOwnProperty(experimentId)) {
                            var bucket = perfTracking[experimentId];
                            if (experimentId && typeof bucket === 'number') {
                                dctk.ewePerformance.addData(experimentId, bucket.toString());
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        }
        if (perfTracking) {
            trackExperiments(perfTracking);
        }

    })();
